////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//        Additional entries to CTRL_PROP_TAB
//
//        CV216/316MZ            Push to Open        ePUSHCLOSE_False
//        CV216/316RGA        Push to Open
//        CV206/306GG            Push to Open
//        CV216/316GG            Push to Open
//
//        CV216,225,240 E,S    Push to Close        ePUSHCLOSE_True
//        CV316,325,340 E,S    Push to Open
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//        Table CTRL_PROP_TAB : Control properties
//
//    new:CDB_ControlProperties(ID) -> CTRL_PROP_TAB
//    {
//        Number of ports of the control valve. Can be #eCV2W3W_CVNU, eCV2W3W_CV2W, eCV2W3W_CV3W, eCV2W3W_CV4W or eCV2W3W_CV6W.
//        Control valve type. Can be #eCVFUNC_NoControl, #eCVFUNC_ControlOnly, #eCVFUNC_Presettable, #eCVFUNC_PresetPT or #eCVFUNC_Electronic.
//        Control characteristic. Can be #eCTRLCHAR_NotChar, #eCTRLCHAR_Linear or #eCTRLCHAR_EqualPc.
//        Mixing or dividing mode. Can be #eMIXDIV_None, #eMIXDIV_Mixing or #eMIXDIV_Dividing.
//        Push or pull to close. Can be #ePUSHCLOSE_Undef, #ePUSHCLOSE_False or #ePUSHCLOSE_True.
//        BCV type. Can be #eBcvType_None, #eBcvType_KvSeries, #eBcvType_LiftLimit, #eBcvType_CharIndep or #eBcvType_Electronic.
//    }
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
new:CDB_ControlProperties(CP_MULTI\1) -> CTRL_PROP_TAB
{
    #eCV2W3W_CV2W                            // Number of ports of the control valve. Can be #eCV2W3W_CVNU, eCV2W3W_CV2W, eCV2W3W_CV3W or eCV2W3W_CV4W.
    #eCVFUNC_ControlOnly                    // Control valve type. Can be #eCVFUNC_NoControl, #eCVFUNC_ControlOnly, #eCVFUNC_Presettable, #eCVFUNC_PresetPT or #eCVFUNC_Electronic.
    #eCTRLCHAR_EqualPc                      // Control characteristic. Can be #eCTRLCHAR_NotChar, #eCTRLCHAR_Linear or #eCTRLCHAR_EqualPc.
    #eMIXDIV_None                           // Mixing or dividing mode. Can be #eMIXDIV_None, #eMIXDIV_Mixing or #eMIXDIV_Dividing.
    #ePUSHCLOSE_True                       // Push or pull to close. Can be #ePUSHCLOSE_Undef, #ePUSHCLOSE_False or #ePUSHCLOSE_True.
    #eBcvType_None                          // BCV type. Can be #eBcvType_None, #eBcvType_KvSeries, #eBcvType_LiftLimit, #eBcvType_CharIndep or #eBcvType_Electronic.
}

new:CDB_ControlProperties(CP_2x6MZ_GG_RGA\1) -> CTRL_PROP_TAB
{
    #eCV2W3W_CV2W                            // Number of ports of the control valve. Can be #eCV2W3W_CVNU, eCV2W3W_CV2W, eCV2W3W_CV3W or eCV2W3W_CV4W.
    #eCVFUNC_ControlOnly                    // Control valve type. Can be #eCVFUNC_NoControl, #eCVFUNC_ControlOnly, #eCVFUNC_Presettable, #eCVFUNC_PresetPT or #eCVFUNC_Electronic.
    #eCTRLCHAR_EqualPc                      // Control characteristic. Can be #eCTRLCHAR_NotChar, #eCTRLCHAR_Linear or #eCTRLCHAR_EqualPc.
    #eMIXDIV_None                           // Mixing or dividing mode. Can be #eMIXDIV_None, #eMIXDIV_Mixing or #eMIXDIV_Dividing.
    #ePUSHCLOSE_False                       // Push or pull to close. Can be #ePUSHCLOSE_Undef, #ePUSHCLOSE_False or #ePUSHCLOSE_True.
    #eBcvType_None                          // BCV type. Can be #eBcvType_None, #eBcvType_KvSeries, #eBcvType_LiftLimit, #eBcvType_CharIndep or #eBcvType_Electronic.
}

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//        Table ACCSERIESRULES : Accessory series exclusion(...) rules
//
//        Rules:
//            ACXXXID \ &ACYYYID   // ACXXXID implies ACYYYID
//            ACXXXID \ !ACYYYID   // ACXXXID excludes ACYYYID
//            >ACXXXID             // ACXXXID is built-in
//            ^ACXXXID             // ACXXXID excludes all others
//		      *ACXXXID			   // ACXXXID two pieces should be included
//			  #ACXXXID			   // ACXXXID is distributed on each parent item (3 vessels (1 primary + 2 secondary) => 3 times the accessory).
//            +ACXXXID             // ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is NOT displayed
//            ++ACXXXID            // ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is displayed
//
//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_RuledTable(ACCSERIESRULES) -> ROOT_TABLE
{
    {
        "Access. series rules"
        0                        // 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
    }
    SER_ACV53 \ !SER_ACV54 \ !SER_ACV55
    SER_ACV54 \ !SER_ACV53 \ !SER_ACV55 \ !SER_ACV57 \ !SER_ACV58
    SER_ACV55 \ !SER_ACV53 \ !SER_ACV54 \ !SER_ACV57 \ !SER_ACV58
    SER_ACV57 \ !SER_ACV54 \ !SER_ACV55 \ !SER_ACV58 \ !SER_ACV59 \ !SER_ACV60 \ !SER_ACV61 
    SER_ACV58 \ !SER_ACV54 \ !SER_ACV55 \ !SER_ACV57 \ !SER_ACV59 \ !SER_ACV60 \ !SER_ACV61
    SER_ACV59 \ !SER_ACV57 \ !SER_ACV58 \ !SER_ACV60
    SER_ACV60 \ !SER_ACV57 \ !SER_ACV58 \ !SER_ACV59
    SER_ACV61 \ !SER_ACV57 \ !SER_ACV58
    SER_ACV66 \ !SER_ACV67 \ !SER_ACV71 \ !SER_ACV72 \ !SER_ACV73 \ !SER_ACV75 \ !SER_ACV76 
    SER_ACV67 \ !SER_ACV66 \ !SER_ACV69 \ !SER_ACV69.1 \ !SER_ACV71 \ !SER_ACV73 \ !SER_ACV75 \ !SER_ACV76 
    SER_ACV69 \ !SER_ACV67 \ !SER_ACV69.1 
    SER_ACV69.1 \ !SER_ACV67 \ !SER_ACV69
    SER_ACV71 \ !SER_ACV66 \ !SER_ACV67 \ !SER_ACV72 \ !SER_ACV73 \ !SER_ACV74 \ !SER_ACV75 \ !SER_ACV76 
    SER_ACV72 \ !SER_ACV66 \ !SER_ACV71
	SER_ACV73 \ !SER_ACV66 \ !SER_ACV67 \ !SER_ACV71 \ !SER_ACV74 \ !SER_ACV75 \ !SER_ACV76 
	SER_ACV74 \ !SER_ACV71 \ !SER_ACV73 \ !SER_ACV75 \ !SER_ACV76 
	SER_ACV75 \ !SER_ACV66 \ !SER_ACV67 \ !SER_ACV71 \ !SER_ACV73 \ !SER_ACV74 \ !SER_ACV76 
	SER_ACV76 \ !SER_ACV66 \ !SER_ACV67 \ !SER_ACV71 \ !SER_ACV73 \ !SER_ACV74 \ !SER_ACV75 
    SER_ACB1 \ !SER_ACB2
    SER_ATCONS \ !SER_ATCONSCL
    SER_ATCLUTCH \ !SER_ATCONSCL
    SER_ATCONSCL \ !SER_ATCONS \ !SER_ATCLUTCH
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//        Table CTRLVALV_TAB : Control valves
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//    new:CDB_ControlValve(ID)->BALCTRLVALV_TAB
//    {
//        {
//            {
//                {
//                    {
//                        {
//                            0                isDeleted
//                            1                isAvailable
//                            0                isHidden
//                            1                isFix
//                            0                Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//                            0                Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
//                             0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//                        }
//                        Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//                        PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//                        Tmax in °C
//                        Tmin in °C
//                    }
//                    "Reference"                Reference to the TA Product
//                    "Name"                    Name of the product
//                    TypeID                    Identifier of the valve type
//                    FamilyID                Identifier of the family of the product
//                    VersionID                Identifier of the version of the product
//                    PriorityLevel            Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//                    Comment                    Product comment
//                    ProdImgID                Product image ID
//                    AccessGroupID            Identifier of the accessory group
//                    PartOfaSet                Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
//                    TableSetID                Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//                    Price                    Price of the product
//                     ProductUseFlag            #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//                    AccessorySeriesID        Identifier of the series of the accessory
//                    isAttached                0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately        
//                   AccTypeID                Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//                    AccFamilyID                Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//                }
//                BodyMaterialID            Identifier of the body material
//                SizeID                    Identifier of the corresp. valve size
//                ConnectID                Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
//                ConnTabID                Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
//                Conn2ID                    Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
//                CBIType                    Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
//                CBISize                    Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
//                CBISizeInch                Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
//                CBICompatibilityIndex    CBI compatibility Index
//                CBIVersion                CBI Version
//                Dpmax                    Maximum Dp of the valve
//                MeasPt                    Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
//                MeasurableData            Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
//                InletSizeID                Identifier of the inlet size ID
//                OutletSizeID            Identifier of the outlet size ID
//            }
//            CharactID        Identifier of the valve characteristic
//        }
//        Kvs                    Kvs of the CV
//        Stroke                Stroke of the CV
//        Rangeability        Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
//        LeakageRate            Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
//        CloseOffCharID        Identifier of the close-off characteristic
//        ActuatorGroupID        Identifier of the actuator group
//        CvAdapterGroupID    Identifier of the CV adapter group
//        CtrlPropID            Identifier of the control properties
//        AdapterListMode        Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
//                            (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
//    }
// Inherited Fields
//    CDB_Thing::Deleted
//    CDB_Thing::Available
//    CDB_Thing::Hidden
//    CDB_Thing::Fixed
//    CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//  CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//    CDB_Thing::SortInt
//    CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//    CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//    CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//    CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//    CDB_Product::Reference
//    CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//    CDB_Product::FamilyID
//    CDB_Product::VersionID
//    CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//    CDB_Product::Comment
//    CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//    CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//    CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//    CDB_Product::Price
//    CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//    CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//    CDB_Product::isAttached
//    CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//    CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//    CDB_TAProduct::BodyMaterialID
//    CDB_TAProduct::SizeID
//    CDB_TAProduct::ConnectID
//    CDB_TAProduct::ConnTabID
//    CDB_TAProduct::Conn2ID
//    CDB_TAProduct::CBIType
//    CDB_TAProduct::CBISize
//    CDB_TAProduct::CBISizeInch
//  CDB_TAProduct::CBICompatibilityIndex
//    CDB_TAProduct::CBIVersion
//    CDB_TAProduct::Dpmax
//    CDB_TAProduct::MeasPt
//    CDB_TAProduct::MeasurableData
//    CDB_TAProduct::InletSizeID
//    CDB_TAProduct::OutletSizeID
//    CDB_RegulatingValve::CharactID
//    CDB_ControlValve::Kvs
//    CDB_ControlValve::Stroke
//    CDB_ControlValve::Rangeability
//    CDB_ControlValve::LeakageRate
//    CDB_ControlValve::CloseOffCharID
//    CDB_ControlValve::ActuatorGroupID
//    CDB_ControlValve::CvAdapterGroupID
//    CDB_ControlValve::CtrlPropID
//    CDB_ControlValve::AdapterListMode
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_ControlValve(MULTI15A_CV) -> CTRLVALV_TAB
{
    {
        {
            {
                {
                    {
                        0                                                // isDeleted
                        1                                               // isAvailable
                        0                                               // isHidden
                        1                                               // isFix
                        0                                                // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
                        0                                                // Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
                          0                                               // Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
                    }
                    1.6e+6 \ 1.6e+6                                     // Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
                    NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
                    120.0                                               // Tmax in °C
                    -10.0                                               // Tmin in °C
                }
                "5850-02.000"                                              // Reference to the TA Product
                "TA-Multi 15"                                           // Name of the product
                CVTYPE_GLOBE                                               // Identifier of the valve type
                FAM_MULTI_CV                                            // Identifier of the family of the product
                VERS_STD                                                // Identifier of the version of the product
                1                                                       // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
                ""                                                      // Product comment
                "PX_TAMULTI20_CV"                                       // Product image ID
                ACCREGVGR_MULTIBV15_FT                                  // Identifier of the accessory group
                #ePartOfaSetNo                                          // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
                NO_ID                                                    // Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
                0.0                                                     // Price of the product
                #eProduct                                               // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
                NO_ID                                                   // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
                0                                                       // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
                NO_ID                                                   // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
                NO_ID                                                    // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth    
            }
            BDY_GUNMETAL                                                  // Identifier of the body material
            DN_15                                                       // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
            CONN_THREAD                                                 // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
            NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
            NO_ID                                                       // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
            ""                                                             // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                                             // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                                            // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
            1                                                           // CBI compatibility Index
            ""                                                            // CBI Version
            2.0e+5                                                      // Maximum Dp of the valve
            #eMeasPointInlet | #eMeasPointMeasStatOut                   // Measuring points
            #eMeasDataDpSignal | #eMeasDataFlow                         // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
            NO_ID                                                        // Identifier of the inlet size ID
            NO_ID                                                        // Identifier of the outlet size ID
        }
        C_MULTI_BV_15                                                     // Identifier of the valve characteristic
    }
    1.88                                               // Kvs of the CV
    4.8e-3                                          // Stroke of the CV
    13.33                                           // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
    0.0002                                          // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
    COC_MULTI                                       // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
    ACTGR_TAMULTI                                   // Identifier of the actuator group
    NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the CV adapter group
    CP_MULTI                                         // Identifier of the control properties
    #eCVAdapterListNA                               // Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                    // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
}

    0.63                                            // Kvs of the CV
    1.2e-2                                          // Stroke of the CV
    50.0                                            // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
    0.0                                             // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
    COC_15B                                         // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
    ACTGR_55-100+FS                                 // Identifier of the actuator group
    NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the CV adapter group
    CP_2x6MZ_GG_RGA                                 // Identifier of the control properties
    #eCVAdapterListNA                               // Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                    // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
}

                    NO_ID                                           // PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
                    150.0                                           // Tmax in °C
                    -15.0                                           // Tmin in °C

                "PX_CV216RGA_15_25"                             // Product image ID

                NO_ID                                            // Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
                0.0                                             // Price of the product

                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)

                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth

                        0                                                // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
                        0                                                // Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
                          0                                               // Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
                    }
                    6.0e+5 \ 6.0e+5                                    // Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
                    NO_ID                                           // PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
                    150.0                                           // Tmax in °C
                    -10.0                                           // Tmin in °C
                }
                "60215-115"                                      // Reference to the TA Product
                "CV 206 GG DN15"                                // Name of the product
                CVTYPE_GLOBE                                    // Identifier of the valve type
                FAM_206GG                                       // Identifier of the family of the product
                VERS_STD                                        // Identifier of the version of the product
                1                                               // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
                ""                                              // Product comment
                "PX_CV206GG_15"                                 // Product image ID
                ACVGR_GG15                                      // Identifier of the accessory group
                #ePartOfaSetNo                                  // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
                NO_ID                                            // Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
                0.0                                             // Price of the product
                #eProduct                                       // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
                0                                               // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
                NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth    
            }
            BDY_CASTIRON                                    // Identifier of the body material
            DN_15                                           // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
            CONN_FLANGE                                     // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
            ""                                              // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
            0                                               // CBI compatibility Index
            ""                                              // CBI Version
            0.0                                             // Maximum Dp of the valve
            #eMeasPointNone                                 // Measuring points
            #eMeasDataNone                                  // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the inlet size ID
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the outlet size ID
        }
        NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the valve characteristic
    }
    0.63                                            // Kvs of the CV

    0.0                                             // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs

////////////////////
// *** CV 216 GG ***
////////////////////

new:CDB_ControlValve(216GG_15A) -> CTRLVALV_TAB
{
    {
        {
            {
                {
                    {
                        0                                                // isDeleted
                        1                                               // isAvailable
                        0                                               // isHidden
                        1                                               // isFix
                        0                                                // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
                        0                                                // Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
                          0                                               // Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
                    }
                    1.6e+6 \ 1.6e+6                                    // Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
                    NO_ID                                           // PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
                    150.0                                           // Tmax in °C
                    -10.0                                           // Tmin in °C
                }
                "60235-115"                                        // Reference to the TA Product
                "CV 216 GG DN15"                                // Name of the product
                CVTYPE_GLOBE                                    // Identifier of the valve type
                FAM_216GG                                       // Identifier of the family of the product
                VERS_STD                                        // Identifier of the version of the product
                1                                               // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
                ""                                              // Product comment
                "PX_CV216GG_15"                                 // Product image ID
                ACVGR_GG15                                      // Identifier of the accessory group
                #ePartOfaSetNo                                  // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
                NO_ID                                            // Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
                0.0                                             // Price of the product
                #eProduct                                       // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
                0                                               // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
                NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth    
            }
            BDY_CASTIRON                                    // Identifier of the body material
            DN_15                                           // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
            CONN_FLANGE                                     // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
            ""                                              // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
            0                                               // CBI compatibility Index
            ""                                              // CBI Version
            0.0                                             // Maximum Dp of the valve
            #eMeasPointNone                                 // Measuring points
            #eMeasDataNone                                  // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the inlet size ID
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the outlet size ID
        }
        NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the valve characteristic
    }
    0.63                                            // Kvs of the CV
    1.4e-2                                          // Stroke of the CV
    50.0                                            // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
    0.0                                             // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
    COC_15B                                         // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
    ACTGR_55-100+FS                                 // Identifier of the actuator group
    NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the CV adapter group
    CP_2x6MZ_GG_RGA                                 // Identifier of the control properties
    #eCVAdapterListNA                               // Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                    // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
}

new:CDB_ControlValve(216_125A) -> CTRLVALV_TAB
{
    {
        {
            {
                {
                    {
                        0                                                // isDeleted
                        1                                               // isAvailable
                        0                                               // isHidden
                        1                                               // isFix
                        0                                                // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
                        0                                                // Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
                          0                                               // Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
                    }
                    1.6e+6 \ 1.6e+6                                    // Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
                    NO_ID                                           // PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
                    180.0                                           // Tmax in °C
                    0.0                                             // Tmin in °C
                }
                "60236-191"                                        // Reference to the TA Product
                "CV 216 DN125"                                  // Name of the product
                CVTYPE_GLOBEIND                                 // Identifier of the valve type
                FAM_216                                         // Identifier of the family of the product
                VERS_STD                                        // Identifier of the version of the product
                1                                               // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
                ""                                              // Product comment
                "PX_CV216_125"                                  // Product image ID
                ACVGR_2XX125                                    // Identifier of the accessory group
                #ePartOfaSetNo                                  // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
                NO_ID                                            // Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
                0.0                                             // Price of the product
                #eProduct                                       // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
                0                                               // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
                NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth    
            }
            BDY_CASTIRON                                    // Identifier of the body material
            DN_125                                          // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
            CONN_FLANGE                                     // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
            ""                                              // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
            0                                               // CBI compatibility Index
            ""                                              // CBI Version
            0.0                                             // Maximum Dp of the valve
            #eMeasPointNone                                 // Measuring points
            #eMeasDataNone                                  // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the inlet size ID
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the outlet size ID
        }
        NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the valve characteristic
    }
    125.0                                            // Kvs of the CV
    6.0e-2                                          // Stroke of the CV
    50.0                                            // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
    0.0001                                          // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
    COC_125D                                        // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
    ACTGR_403-1503                                  // Identifier of the actuator group
    NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the CV adapter group
    CP_2XX                                          // Identifier of the control properties
    #eCVAdapterListNA                               // Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                    // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
}

    50.0                                            // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
    0.0001                                          // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
    COC_15D2                                        // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
    ACTGR_103-503                                   // Identifier of the actuator group
    NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the CV adapter group
    CP_2XX                                          // Identifier of the control properties
    #eCVAdapterListNA                               // Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                    // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
}

new:CDB_ControlValve(240S_15A) -> CTRLVALV_TAB
{
    {
        {
            {
                {
                    {
                        0                                                // isDeleted
                        1                                               // isAvailable
                        0                                               // isHidden
                        1                                               // isFix
                        0                                                // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
                        0                                                // Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
                          0                                               // Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
                    }
                    4.0e+6 \ 4.0e+6                                    // Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
                    NO_ID                                           // PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
                    180.0                                           // Tmax in °C
                    0.0                                             // Tmin in °C
                }
                "60258-115"                                        // Reference to the TA Product
                "CV 240S DN15"                                  // Name of the product
                CVTYPE_GLOBEIND                                 // Identifier of the valve type
                FAM_240S                                        // Identifier of the family of the product
                VERS_STD                                        // Identifier of the version of the product
                1                                               // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
                ""                                              // Product comment
                "PX_CV225_240S_E_15"                            // Product image ID
                ACVGR_2XX15                                     // Identifier of the accessory group
                #ePartOfaSetNo                                  // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
                NO_ID                                            // Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
                0.0                                             // Price of the product
                #eProduct                                       // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
                0                                               // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
                NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth    
            }
            BDY_CASTSTEEL                                    // Identifier of the body material
            DN_15                                           // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
            CONN_FLANGE                                     // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
            ""                                              // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
            0                                               // CBI compatibility Index
            ""                                              // CBI Version
            0.0                                             // Maximum Dp of the valve
            #eMeasPointNone                                 // Measuring points
            #eMeasDataNone                                  // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the inlet size ID
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the outlet size ID
        }
        NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the valve characteristic
    }
    0.16                                            // Kvs of the CV
    2.0e-2                                          // Stroke of the CV
    50.0                                            // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
    0.0001                                          // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
    COC_15D2                                        // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
    ACTGR_103-503                                   // Identifier of the actuator group
    NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the CV adapter group
    CP_2XX                                          // Identifier of the control properties
    #eCVAdapterListNA                               // Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                    // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
}

new:CDB_ControlValve(240E_15A) -> CTRLVALV_TAB
{
    {
        {
            {
                {
                    {
                        0                                                // isDeleted
                        1                                               // isAvailable
                        0                                               // isHidden
                        1                                               // isFix
                        0                                                // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
                        0                                                // Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
                          0                                               // Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
                    }
                    4.0e+6 \ 4.0e+6                                    // Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
                    NO_ID                                           // PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
                    180.0                                           // Tmax in °C
                    0.0                                             // Tmin in °C
                }
                "60259-115"                                        // Reference to the TA Product
                "CV 240E DN15"                                  // Name of the product
                CVTYPE_GLOBEIND                                 // Identifier of the valve type
                FAM_240E                                        // Identifier of the family of the product
                VERS_STD                                        // Identifier of the version of the product
                1                                               // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
                ""                                              // Product comment
                "PX_CV225_240S_E_15"                            // Product image ID
                ACVGR_240E15                                    // Identifier of the accessory group
                #ePartOfaSetNo                                  // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
                NO_ID                                            // Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
                0.0                                             // Price of the product
                #eProduct                                       // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
                0                                               // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
                NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth    
            }
            BDY_STSTEEL                                        // Identifier of the body material
            DN_15                                           // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
            CONN_FLANGE                                     // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
            ""                                              // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
            0                                               // CBI compatibility Index
            ""                                              // CBI Version
            0.0                                             // Maximum Dp of the valve
            #eMeasPointNone                                 // Measuring points
            #eMeasDataNone                                  // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the inlet size ID
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the outlet size ID
        }
        NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the valve characteristic
    }
    0.16                                            // Kvs of the CV
    2.0e-2                                          // Stroke of the CV
    50.0                                            // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
    0.0001                                          // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
    COC_15D2                                        // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
    ACTGR_103-503                                   // Identifier of the actuator group
    NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the CV adapter group
    CP_2XX                                          // Identifier of the control properties
    #eCVAdapterListNA                               // Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                    // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
}

////////////////
// *** V20xx ***
// Brazilian specific
// Remark: there is no article number for these valves because there are only sold by set with their actuators
////////////////

new:CDB_ControlValve(V20_15B) -> CTRLVALV_TAB
{
    {
        {
            {
                {
                    {
                        0                                                // isDeleted
                        1                                               // isAvailable
                        0                                               // isHidden
                        1                                               // isFix
                        0                                                // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
                        0                                                // Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
                          0                                               // Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
                    }
                    0.6e+6 \ 2.5e+6                                    // Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
                    NO_ID                                           // PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
                    120.0                                           // Tmax in °C
                    0.0                                             // Tmin in °C
                }
                "-"                                                // Reference to the TA Product
                "V2015B 1/2""                                   // Name of the product
                CVTYPE_BALL                                     // Identifier of the valve type
                FAM_TAV2                                        // Identifier of the family of the product
                VERS_STD                                        // Identifier of the version of the product
                1                                               // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
                ""                                              // Product comment
                "TA_2WCV_M"                                     // Product image ID
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the accessory group
                #ePartOfaSetYes                                 // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
                CVACTSET_TAB                                    // Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
                0.0                                             // Price of the product
                #eProduct                                       // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
                0                                               // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
                NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
                NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth    
            }
            BDY_BRONZE                                        // Identifier of the body material
            DN_15                                           // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
            CONN_THREADN                                    // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
            NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
            ""                                              // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
            ""                                              // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
            0                                               // CBI compatibility Index
            ""                                              // CBI Version
            0.0                                             // Maximum Dp of the valve
            #eMeasPointNone                                 // Measuring points
            #eMeasDataNone                                  // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the inlet size ID
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the outlet size ID
        }
        NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the valve characteristic
    }
    4.0                                                // Kvs of the CV
    90.0                                            // Stroke of the CV
    50.0                                            // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
    0.0                                             // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
    COC_V2015-25                                    // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
    ACTGR_MF424                                     // Identifier of the actuator group
    NO_ID                                           // Identifier of the CV adapter group
    CP_TAV2                                         // Identifier of the control properties
    #eCVAdapterListNA                               // Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                                    // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
}

new:CDB_ControlValve(V20_20C) -> CTRLVALV_TAB
{    Inherited(V20_15B)
    {
        CDB_Product::Name            =    "V2020C 3/4""
        CDB_TAProduct::SizeID        =    DN_20
        CDB_ControlValve::Kvs        =    6.30
    }

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//        Table 6WAYCTRLVALV_TAB : 6 way ctrl valves
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//    new:CDB_6WayValve(ID)->6WAYCTRLVALV_TAB
//    {
//        {
//            {
//                {
//                    {
//                        {
//                            {
//                                0                isDeleted
//                                1                isAvailable
//                                0                isHidden
//                                1                isFix
//                                0                Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//                                0                Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
//                              0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//                            }
//                            Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//                            PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//                            Tmax in °C
//                            Tmin in °C
//                        }
//                        "Reference"                Reference to the TA Product
//                        "Name"                    Name of the product
//                        TypeID                    Identifier of the valve type
//                        FamilyID                Identifier of the family of the product
//                        VersionID                Identifier of the version of the product
//                        PriorityLevel            Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//                        Comment                    Product comment
//                        ProdImgID                Product image ID
//                        AccessGroupID            Identifier of the accessory group
//                        PartOfaSet                Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
//                        TableSetID                Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//                        Price                    Price of the product
//                         ProductUseFlag            #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//                        AccessorySeriesID        Identifier of the series of the accessory
//                        isAttached                0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately        
//                       AccTypeID                Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//                        AccFamilyID                Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//                    }
//                    BodyMaterialID            Identifier of the body material
//                    SizeID                    Identifier of the corresp. valve size
//                    ConnectID                Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
//                    ConnTabID                Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
//                    Conn2ID                    Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
//                    CBIType                    Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
//                    CBISize                    Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
//                    CBISizeInch                Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
//                    CBICompatibilityIndex    CBI compatibility Index
//                    CBIVersion                CBI Version
//                    Dpmax                    Maximum Dp of the valve
//                    MeasPt                    Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
//                    MeasurableData            Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
//                    InletSizeID                Identifier of the inlet size ID
//                    OutletSizeID            Identifier of the outlet size ID
//                }
//                CharactID                // MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in PICVCharID
//            }
//            Kvs                        Kvs of the CV (Kvs is the Kv at full opening)
//            Stroke                    Stroke of the CV
//            Rangeability            Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
//            LeakageRate                Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
//            CloseOffCharID            Identifier of the close-off characteristic
//            ActuatorGroupID            Identifier of the actuator group
//            CvAdapterGroupID        Identifier of the CV adapter group
//             CtrlPropID                Identifier of the control properties
//            AdapterListMode            Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
//                                    (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
//        }
//        6WayQmax                Maximum flow rate across the valve
//        PicvGroupID                Table that contains IDs of PIBCV that can be used with this 6 way valve
//        BvFamiliesGroupID        Table that contains IDs of all the BV family IDs that can be used with this 6 way valve
//    }
// Inherited Fields
//    CDB_Thing::Deleted
//    CDB_Thing::Available
//    CDB_Thing::Hidden
//    CDB_Thing::Fixed
//    CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//    CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//    CDB_Thing::SortInt
//    CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//    CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//    CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//    CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//    CDB_Product::Reference
//    CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//    CDB_Product::FamilyID
//    CDB_Product::VersionID
//    CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//    CDB_Product::Comment
//    CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//    CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//    CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//    CDB_Product::Price
//    CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//    CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//    CDB_Product::isAttached
//    CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//    CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//    CDB_TAProduct::BodyMaterialID
//    CDB_TAProduct::SizeID
//    CDB_TAProduct::ConnectID
//    CDB_TAProduct::ConnTabID
//    CDB_TAProduct::Conn2ID
//    CDB_TAProduct::CBIType
//    CDB_TAProduct::CBISize
//    CDB_TAProduct::CBISizeInch
//  CDB_TAProduct::CBICompatibilityIndex
//    CDB_TAProduct::CBIVersion
//    CDB_TAProduct::Dpmax
//    CDB_TAProduct::MeasPt
//    CDB_TAProduct::MeasurableData
//    CDB_TAProduct::InletSizeID
//    CDB_TAProduct::OutletSizeID
//    CDB_RegulatingValve::CharactID
//    CDB_ControlValve::Kvs
//    CDB_ControlValve::Stroke
//    CDB_ControlValve::Rangeability
//    CDB_ControlValve::LeakageRate
//    CDB_ControlValve::CloseOffCharID
//    CDB_ControlValve::ActuatorGroupID
//    CDB_ControlValve::CvAdapterGroupID
//    CDB_ControlValve::CtrlPropID
//    CDB_ControlValve::AdapterListMode
//  CDB_6WayValve::Qmax
//  CDB_6WayValve::PicvGroupID
//  CDB_6WayValve::BvFamiliesGroupID
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_6WayValve(6WAY_STD_FLAT_15) -> 6WAYCTRLVALV_TAB
{
    {
        {
            {
                {
                    {
                        {
                            0                                                    // isDeleted
                            1                                                   // isAvailable
                            0                                                   // isHidden
                            1                                                   // isFix
                            1                                                   // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
                            0                                                   // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
                            0                                                   // Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
                        }
                        0.6e+6 \ 1.6e+6                                     // Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
                        NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID            Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
                        120.0                                               // Tmax in °C
                        -10.0                                               // Tmin in °C
                    }
                    "322203-13000"                                         // Reference to the TA Product
                    "IDS_NAME_6WAYVALVE_DN15"                              // Name of the product
                    6WAYTYPE_CO                                            // Identifier of the valve type
                    FAM_6WAY_VALVE                                      // Identifier of the family of the product
                    VERS_NCKLPLATED                                     // Identifier of the version of the product
                    1                                                   // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
                    ""                                                  // Product comment
                    "NO_ID"                                               // Product image ID
                    ACVGR_TA6WAYVFLAT                                   // Identifier of the accessory group
                    #ePartOfaSetNo                                      // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
                    NO_ID                                                // Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
                    0.0                                                 // Price of the product
                    #eProduct                                              // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
                    NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
                    0                                                   // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
                    NO_ID                                                  // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
                    NO_ID                                                // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth    
                }
                BDY_DZR                                             // Identifier of the body material
                DN_15                                               // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
                CONN_FLATFACED_THRM                                 // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
                NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
                NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
                ""                                                    // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
                ""                                                  // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
                ""                                                     // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
                0                                                   // CBI compatibility Index
                ""                                                    // CBI Version
                2e+5                                                // Maximum Dp of the valve
                #eMeasPointNone                                        // Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
                #eMeasDataNone                                       // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
                CONSIZE_MG3_4                                        // Identifier of the inlet size ID
                CONSIZE_MG3_4                                        // Identifier of the outlet size ID
            }
            NO_ID                                            // Identifier of the valve characteristic
        }
        1.25                                                // Kvs of the CV
        -1                                                    // Stroke of the CV
        0.0                                                    // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
        0.0                                                    // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
        NO_ID                                                // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
        ACTGR_6WAY_1520                                        // Identifier of the actuator group
        NO_ID                                                // Identifier of the CV adapter group
        CP_6Way                                                // Identifier of the control properties
        #eCVAdapterListNA                                   // Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
    }
    5.013888889E-04                                // 1805 l/h; Maximum flow rate accross the valve (m3/s)
    6WAYV_PICV_TAB                                 // Table that contains IDs of PIBCV that can be used with this 6 way valve in EQM mode.
    6WAYV_BVFAM_TAB                                // Table that contains IDs of all the BV family IDs that can be used with this 6 way valve
}

//////////////////////////////
// Compatibility table for 6-way valve selection
// This table contains for each circuit type, the power supply and input signal for the 
// actuator that are compatible with the 6-way valve.
//////////////////////////////

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//                                CDB_6WayValveActuatorCompatibility
//
//    Inherited from CDB_StringArray
//
//    {
//        n                                    // Number of column of the selection.
//        str1 \ str2 \ str3 .. \ strn        // array of string contains data in strng format
//        str'1 \ str'2 \ str'3 .. \ str'n
//        ...
//    }
//
//  n = 4
//   str1 = Enum that describes the type of circuit used with the 6-way valve.
//   str2 = Power supply ID list for actuator compatible with 6-way valve.
//     remark: You can put more that one power supply ID with '|' as separator.
//   str3 = Input signal ID list for actuator compatible with 6-way valve.
//     remark: You can put more that one input signal ID with '|' as separator.
//   str4 = Family ID for actuator compatibles with PIBCV valve.
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
new:CDB_6WayValveActuatorCompatibility(6WAY_ACTR_COMP) -> ROOT_TABLE
{
    {
        4
        #e6Way_Alone \ POW_24VAC|POW_230VAC \ SIG_3POINT|SIG_0-10V|SIG_10-0V|SIG_2-10V|SIG_10-2V \ NO_ID
        #e6Way_EQMControl \ POW_24VAC \ SIG_3POINT \ ACTFAM_SLIDER
        #e6Way_OnOffControlWithPIBCV \ POW_24VAC|POW_230VAC \ SIG_3POINT|SIG_0-10V|SIG_10-0V|SIG_2-10V|SIG_10-2V \ NO_ID
        #e6Way_OnOffControlWithSTAD \ POW_24VAC|POW_230VAC \ SIG_3POINT|SIG_0-10V|SIG_10-0V|SIG_2-10V|SIG_10-2V \ NO_ID
    }
}

//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
// HYS-1877: Add US Kits for TA-6-way valves. 
// We create NextID field to do the union between 6-way valve + actuator and PIBCV + actuator
//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
// Table 6WAYCTRLVALVSET_TAB : TA-6-way valve, TA-M106 CO actuator,
// TA-COMPACT-P valve incl tailpieces, TA-Slider 160 CO actuator
// When reading CDB_Set object (txt file) TAS4 will update
// First and Second ID, TA_Product::PartOfASet member variable
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	new:CDB_Set(ID)->6WAYCTRLVALVSET_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			0				isDeleted
//			1				isAvailable
//			0				isHidden
//			1				isFix
//			0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//			0				Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
//      	0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//		}
//		"Reference"			Reference to the TA Product
//		"Name"				Name of the product
//		FirstID				Identifier of the control valve
//		SecondID			Identifier of the actuator
//		AccessGroupID		Identifier of the accessory group
//		"Parameter"			String to allow to apply some filter.
//		"NextID"			Identifier of the next ID to consider can be Set ID, Group ID, Product ID etc...
//	}
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SorTInt
//	CDB_Set::Reference
//	CDB_Set::Name
//	CDB_Set::FirstID
//	CDB_Set::SecondID
//	CDB_Set::AccGroupID
//	CDB_Set::Parameter
//	CDB_Set::NextID
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

		0														// isDeleted
		1                                                       // isAvailable
		0                                                       // isHidden
		1                                                       // isFix
		0                                                       // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
		0                                                       // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
		0               										// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
	}
	"339010-50400"											// Reference to the TA Product
	"IDS_NAME_6WAYVALVE_KIT1"                               // Name of the product
